        <script type='text/javascript'>
            var todayDateTime = "2024/09/19 07:44:45";
            var MobileData_LS = "mobile_data_" + menu_version_local_storage;
            var TabletDataFooter_LS = "tablet_footer_" + menu_version_local_storage;
            var allData = '';
            window.onload = function removeHoverSubMenu() {
                const navEle = document.getElementById('hover_nav');
                if (typeof (navEle) != 'undefined' && navEle != null) {
                    navEle.removeAttribute('id');
                }
            }
            function createCookie(name, value, days) {
                if (days) {
                    var date = new Date();
                    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                    var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
                } else
                    var expires = "";
                document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
            }
            function readCookie(name) {
                var nameEQ = name + "=";
                var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
                        c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
                        return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
                }
                return null;
            }
            function addListElements(head_txt, head_category_name) {
                var list = '';
            }
            function getXMLHttpRequestObject() {
                var xmlhttp;
                if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
                    xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
                } else {
                    xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
                }
                return xmlhttp;
            }
            function subHeaderDataFooter() {
                if (window.localStorage && (tablets_data_footer = window.localStorage.getItem(TabletDataFooter_LS)) && tablets_data_footer != "") {
                    document.getElementById('otherData').innerHTML += tablets_data_footer;
                } else {
                    loadFromAjaxTabletsFooterData();
                }
            }
            function loadFromAjaxMobilesData(obj) {
                window.localStorage.removeItem(MobileData_LS);
                var xmlhttp = getXMLHttpRequestObject();
                xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
                    if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4) {
                        if (xmlhttp.status == 200) {
                            window.localStorage.setItem(MobileData_LS, xmlhttp.responseText);
                            allData = xmlhttp.responseText;
                            addDataToSubHeader(obj, allData);
                        } else if (xmlhttp.status == 400) {} else {}
                    }
                }
                xmlhttp.open("POST", "/template/common/sub_header_data.php?ord=" + Math.random() + "&category=mobile_data&categoryId=553", true);
                xmlhttp.send();
            }
            function loadFromAjaxTabletsFooterData() {
                var xmlhttp = getXMLHttpRequestObject();
                xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
                    if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4) {
                        if (xmlhttp.status == 200) {
                            allData = xmlhttp.responseText;
                            window.localStorage.setItem(TabletDataFooter_LS, xmlhttp.responseText);
                            document.getElementById('otherData').innerHTML += allData;
                        } else if (xmlhttp.status == 400) {} else {}
                    }
                }
                xmlhttp.open("POST", "/template/common/sub_header_data.php?category=other&categoryId=553", true);
                xmlhttp.send();
            }
            function mobileData(obj, category_id) {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    if (window.localStorage && (mobiles_data = window.localStorage.getItem(MobileData_LS)) && mobiles_data != "") {
                        var htmlObject = document.createElement('div');
                        htmlObject.innerHTML = mobiles_data;
                        obj.innerHTML = htmlObject.innerHTML
                        addContainer();
                        loadSubMenuData();
                    } else {
                        loadFromAjaxMobilesData(obj);
                    }
                }, 0);
            }
            function addDataToSubHeader(obj, data) {
                obj.innerHTML = data;
                addContainer();
                loadSubMenuData();
            }
            ;function addContainer() {
                var aContainer = document.createElement('div');
                aContainer.setAttribute('id', 'overlay_menu');
                aContainer.style.cssText = 'display:none;position:fixed;left: 0; top: 0;bottom: 0;right: 0;opacity: 0.9;width: 100%;height: 100%;filter: alpha(opacity=80);z-index: 9999;background-color:rgba(0,0,0,1)';
                document.body.appendChild(aContainer);
            }
            var timer;
            function loadSubMenuData() {
                var e = document.getElementsByClassName("drowndown_menu");
                (e = [].slice.call(e)).forEach(function(e, l, t) {
                    e.onmouseenter = function(l) {
                        if (timer != null) {
                            clearTimeout(timer);
                        }
                        timer = setTimeout(function() {
                            child_li = e.getElementsByClassName("sub_menu_data");
                            for (var t = document.getElementsByClassName("sub_menu_data"), n = 0; n < t.length; n++)
                                t[n].classList.remove("d-block");
                            child_li[0].classList.add("d-block"),
                            document.getElementById("overlay_menu").style.display = "block"
                        }, 300);
                    }
                    ,
                    e.onmouseleave = function(l) {
                        if (timer != null) {
                            clearTimeout(timer);
                            timer = null;
                        }
                        timer = setTimeout(function() {
                            child_li = e.getElementsByClassName("sub_menu_data")
                            for (var t = document.getElementsByClassName("sub_menu_data"), n = 0; n < t.length; n++)
                                t[n].classList.remove("d-block");
                            child_li[0].classList.remove("d-block"),
                            document.getElementById("overlay_menu").style.display = "none"
                        }, 500)
                    }
                })
            }
            ;if (readCookie('91_home') == null) {
                createCookie('91_home', 1, 30);

                function getCookie(name) {
                    const value = `; ${document.cookie}`;
                    const parts = value.split(`; ${name}=`);
                    if (parts.length === 2)
                        return parts.pop().split(';').shift();
                }
                var dfpGetCookie = getCookie("dfp-imp");
                if (dfpGetCookie != undefined) {

            function googleAdsonScroll() {
                var footer_gad_scroll = true;
                var loadFooterImage = true;
                window.onscroll = function() {
                    if (footer_gad_scroll && document.getElementById('footer_gad') != 'undefined' && document.getElementById('footer_gad') != null) {
                        var rect = document.getElementById('footer_gad').getBoundingClientRect();
                        if (rect.top < window.innerHeight && window.footer_slot_160_600) {
                            refreshGoogleCreativeAds(footer_slot_160_600);
                            footer_gad_scroll = false;
                            //console.log('footer_gad_scroll')
                        }
                    }

                    if (loadFooterImage && window.scrollY >= 500) {
                        initFooterImage();
                        loadFooterImage = false;
                    }
                }
            }
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                googleAdsonScroll();
            });

            function refreshGoogleCreativeAds(ad_slot_id) {
                //console.log(" slot is ="+ad_slot_id)
                googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                    //console.log('called');
                    googletag.pubads().refresh([ad_slot_id]);
                });
            }
            function initFooterImage() {
                var imgBackGroundDefer = document.getElementsByClassName('img_background');
                if (imgBackGroundDefer.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < imgBackGroundDefer.length; i++) {
                        if (imgBackGroundDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src-background')) {
                            imgBackGroundDefer[i].style.backgroundImage = "url('" + imgBackGroundDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src-background' + '') + "')";

                        }
                    }
                }
            }

    var categoryId = '553';
    var productId = '';
    var brandId = '';
    var productPrice = '';
    var IMPRESSION_GTS_TRACKING_API_URL = 'https://tasks.91mobiles.com/nm/api/analytics/desktopEvent';
    var page_id = '';
    var desktopListPageEvent = '';
    var isDetailPage = 'home-page';

    var impressionStatus = {}
      , date = new Date
      , origin = null;
    function checkIfElementInViewPort(e) {
        if (null === e)
            return !1;
        var t = e.getBoundingClientRect()
          , o = e.offsetHeight
          , i = window.innerHeight;
        return t.top >= 0 && t.top <= i || t.bottom >= 0 && t.bottom <= o
    }
    function getParameterByName(e, t) {
        e = e.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
        var o = new RegExp("[?&]" + e + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)").exec(t);
        return o ? o[2] ? decodeURIComponent(o[2].replace(/\+/g, " ")) : "" : null
    }
    function trackImpressionsAndGts1(e) {
        var t = JSON.stringify(e)
          , o = new XMLHttpRequest;
        o.open("POST", IMPRESSION_GTS_TRACKING_API_URL, !0),
        o.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/json"),
        o.setRequestHeader("source", "web"),
        o.onreadystatechange = function() {
            4 == o.readyState && o.status
        }
        ,
        o.send(t)
    }
    function checkImpressionStatus(e, t, o, i) {
        return !!impressionStatus[e + "sept" + t + "sept" + o + "sept" + i] && impressionStatus[e + "sept" + t + "sept" + o + "sept" + i].status
    }
    function setImpressionStatus(e, t, o, i, n) {
        impressionStatus[e + "sept" + t + "sept" + i + "sept" + n] = {
            status: !0,
            position: o
        }
    }
    function getUserProperties1() {
        var e = decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; __utma=").pop().split(";").shift());
        void 0 !== e && "" !== e && (e = (e = e.split("."))[0] + "." + e[1]);
        var t = decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; PHPSESSID=").pop().split(";").shift());
        t.indexOf("~") >= 0 && (t = t.split("~")[1]);
        var o = decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; fcmid=").pop().split(";").shift());
        return void 0 === o && (o = ""),
        {
            googleId: e,
            sessionId: t,
            fcmId: o,
            userId: document.getElementById("data-uid").textContent ? document.getElementById("data-uid").textContent : null
        }
    }
    function getUserPathData1() {
        if (void 0 !== window.localStorage) {
            var e = decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; userPath=").pop().split(";").shift())
              , t = window.localStorage.getItem("userPath");
            if (t = "string" == typeof t && "" !== t ? JSON.parse(t) : [],
            void 0 !== e && "" !== e) {
                e = JSON.parse(e);
                for (var o in e)
                    t.push(e[o]);
                document.cookie = "userPath =;domain=.91mobiles.com; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/;"
            }
            return window.localStorage.setItem("userPath", JSON.stringify(t)),
            t
        }
        return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; userPath=").pop().split(";").shift()))
    }
    function getImpressionsOnScroll1(e, t, o, i, n) {
        var r = 0
          , s = []
          , a = {}
          , p = [];
        if ("" !== i && "" !== n && "" !== t && "" !== o && "object" == typeof e && null !== e) {
            if (void 0 === (p = e.querySelectorAll(t)) || null === p)
                return;
            if ((p = [].slice.call(p)).forEach(function(e) {
                ++r;
                var t = e.getAttribute("data-store");
                if ("none" !== e.style.display && !checkImpressionStatus(o, t, i, n)) {
                    var a, p = parseInt(e.querySelector("[data-price]").getAttribute("data-price"));
                    null !== origin && "undefined" !== origin || (origin = getParameterByName("origin", e.querySelector("span[data-href-url]").getAttribute("data-href-url")));
                    var c = getParameterByName("outofstock", e.querySelector("span[data-href-url]").getAttribute("data-href-url"));
                    a = {
                        productId: parseInt(productId),
                        catId: parseInt(categoryId),
                        position: r,
                        storeName: t,
                        section: o,
                        storePrice: p,
                        "variant-color": i,
                        "variant-storage": n,
                        outofstock: void 0 === c || null === c ? null : c
                    },
                    s.push(a),
                    setImpressionStatus(o, t, r, i, n)
                }
            }),
            s.length > 0) {
                var c = getUserPathData1()
                  , d = "";
                void 0 !== c && "" !== c ? d = c[c.length - 2] : c = null;
                var l = decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; landingPageUrl=").pop().split(";").shift());
                void 0 !== l && "" !== l || (l = window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
                var u = getUserProperties1();
                a.eventProperties = s,
                a.userProperties = u,
                a.eventName = "impression",
                a.source = "web",
                a.timeStamp = parseInt(date.getTime() / 1e3),
                a.landingPageUrl = l,
                a.lastPageUrl = d,
                a.pageUrlList = c,
                a.pageType = origin,
                trackImpressionsAndGts1(a)
            }
        }
    }
    function checkAndGetImpression1(e) {
        var t = {
            overview: "overview",
            pricelist: "store_prices"
        };
        "string" == typeof e && "" !== e && e in t && (t = {
            sectionToCheck: t[e]
        });
        for (var o in t)
            if (checkIfElementInViewPort(document.getElementById(t[o])))
                switch (o) {
                case "overview":
                    var i = "all"
                      , n = "all"
                      , r = document.getElementById("overview").querySelector('span[data-variant-type="color"]');
                    if ("object" == typeof r && null !== r) {
                        for (var s = r.parentNode; "overview" !== s.id; ) {
                            if ("DIV" === s.tagName && s.className.indexOf("selectBox") > -1) {
                                i = s.value;
                                break
                            }
                            s = s.parentNode
                        }
                        i = "string" != typeof i || "" === i ? "all" : i
                    }
                    getImpressionsOnScroll1(document.getElementById("overviewPriceListDivId"), "div.spec_rvw_pnl", o, i, n);
                    break;
                case "pricelist":
                    i = "all",
                    n = "all";
                    var a = document.getElementById("store_prices").querySelector('span[data-variant-type="color"]');
                    if ("object" == typeof a && null !== a) {
                        for (s = a.parentNode; "store_prices" !== s.id; ) {
                            if ("DIV" === s.tagName && s.className.indexOf("selectBox") > -1) {
                                i = s.value;
                                break
                            }
                            s = s.parentNode
                        }
                        i = "string" != typeof i || "" === i ? "all" : i
                    }
                    var p = document.getElementById("store_prices").querySelector('span[data-variant-type="memory"]');
                    if ("object" == typeof p && null !== p) {
                        for (s = p.parentNode; "store_prices" !== s.id; ) {
                            if ("DIV" === s.tagName && s.className.indexOf("selectBox") > -1) {
                                n = s.value;
                                break
                            }
                            s = s.parentNode
                        }
                        n = "string" != typeof n || "" === n ? "all" : n
                    }
                    getImpressionsOnScroll1(document.getElementById("onlineStoresListRowDivId"), "div.prc_listPanel", o, i, n)
                }
    }
    function checkAndGetImpressionOnPageVisit() {
        var e = []
          , t = {}
          , o = {
            productId: parseInt(productId),
            catId: parseInt(categoryId),
            brandId: parseInt(brandId),
            productPrice: parseInt(productPrice)
        };
        e.push(o);

        void 0 !== i && "" !== i || (i = window.location.pathname + window.location.search),
        t.eventProperties = e,
        t.userProperties = getUserProperties1("onPageVisit"),
        t.eventName = "detailPageVisit",
        t.source = "web",
        t.timeStamp = parseInt((new Date).getTime() / 1e3),
        trackImpressionsAndGts1(t)
    }
    function checkAndGetImpressionOnListPageVisit() {

          , t = JSON.parse(desktopListPageEvent);
        if (t.length > 0)
            for (i = 0; i < t.length; i++)
                e.push(t[i]);

          , n = e
          , r = decodeURIComponent((";" + document.cookie).split("; landingPageUrl=").pop().split(";").shift());
        void 0 !== r && "" !== r || (r = window.location.pathname + window.location.search),

        o.eventName = "listingPageVisit",

    }

<script type='text/javascript'>
    var mini_finder_attr_array = [];
    function set_up_mini_finder_hover(cat_id, cat_name, max_price, attrs) {
        var data = jQuery.makeArray(mini_finder_attr_array);
        if (data == '' || data == null || typeof (data) === undefined || !data[0].hasOwnProperty([cat_id])) {
            return false;
        }
        var chk = 0;
        var current_price = max_price
        if (max_price >= data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'][data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'].length - 2]) {
            current_price = data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'][data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'].length - 2];
            current_price = '';
            chk = 1;
        }
        if (chk == 0) {
            var length = data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'].length;
            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                price = data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'][i];
                if (price) {
                    if (price >= max_price) {
                        if ((price - max_price) <= (max_price - data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'][i - 1])) {
                            current_price = price;
                            i = length + 1;
                        } else {
                            current_price = data[0][cat_id]['max_prices'][i];
                            i = length + 1;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        var att_value = {};
        var length = attrs.length;
        for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
            if (attr[i] == 'top_brands') {
                att_value[attr[i]] = data[0][cat_id]['top_brands'];
            } else {
                att_value[attr[i]] = data[0][cat_id]['segment' + current_price + ':' + attr[i]];
            }
        }
        return att_value;
    }
</script>
